#window 72:2
startswitch {
  set @dummytimer = func_gametime
}

thinkswitch {
  set @deltasource = (func_gametime - @dummytimer)
  if (@deltasource > 50)
    closewindow 72:2
}

finishswitch {
  if (arriving_on_train == 0) {
    console "target barriers"
  } else
    extern playscene hephtower1_leavecar
}

  goto 72:0107
}

style "style_hephaestus"

#window 72:3000
xyprintfx 580, 32, 1, 1, 1, 1, _bigfont, ":0%d", @secsleft
startswitch {
  extern ANIM_MakeSmart @pc
  extern AI_ReleaseEntity @pc
  set @secsleft = 5
  set @touchSuspect = 1
  extern cam_restore
  set @startticks = func_gametime
}

thinkswitch {
  if (@clicked_on_suspect)
    goto 0:0
  if (@not_now)
    goto 0:0
  set @ticksgoneby = (func_gametime - @startticks)
  set @poo = @secsleft
  if (@ticksgoneby > 1000)
    set @secsleft = 4
  if (@ticksgoneby > 2000)
    set @secsleft = 3
  if (@ticksgoneby > 3000)
    set @secsleft = 2
  if (@ticksgoneby > 4000)
    set @secsleft = 1
  if (@ticksgoneby > 4900)
    set @secsleft = 0
  if ((@ticksgoneby > 5000) && (@not_now == 0))
    closewindow 72:3000
  if (@poo != @secsleft)
    extern playsound ui/gen/ui_gen_clocktick.wav
}

finishswitch {
  set @touchSuspect = 0
  extern cam_anoxmariomode 0
  if (suspect_angela == 1) {
    extern cam_from 201.69 1687.19 179.69
    extern cam_to 142.20 1709.85 173.06
  }
  if (suspect_liseria == 1) {
    extern cam_from 189.31 1686.44 187.94
    extern cam_to 139.25 1723.75 173.86
  }
  if (suspect_thomas == 1) {
    extern cam_from 189.19 1693.19 201.81
    extern cam_to 137.89 1724.52 179.82
  }
  if (@close_timer_without_result == 1)
    goto 0:0
  if (suspect_proof)
    goto 72:4100
  goto 72:1530
}

  console "forcecursormode 1"
  extern FlashScreenf 0 0 0 0 0
  extern FlashScreenf 0 0 0 1 1
  set @tstart = func_gametime
  set @flashing = 0
}

thinkswitch {
  set @t = (func_gametime - @tstart)
  if ((@t > 1100) && (@flashing == 0)) {
    gosub 72:8501		                  
    extern cam_from 1530 1481 863
    extern cam_to 1478 1510 839
    extern cam_zip
    extern FlashScreenf 0 0 0 1 0
    extern FlashScreenf 0 0 0 0 2
    set @flashing = 1
  }
  if (@t > 3000) {
    gosub 72:8505
    closewindow 72:8500
  }
}

finishswitch {
  console "forcecursormode 0"
}

startswitch {
  extern AI_SpawnEntity hArrow cursor_cine fatarrow 0:0 fatima_elem1
  set @fatmove_MS = func_gametime
  extern ANIM_PlayAnim grumpos_handle talk_a 0 1 0
  extern AI_WaitAndFace bootshandle -1 grumpos_elem
  extern loopsound battle/character_boots_com/boots_fat_screen_loop.wav
}

thinkswitch {
  if (func_gametime < (@fatmove_MS + 100))
    goto 0:0
  set @fatmove_MS = func_gametime
  extern AI_GetXYZ hArrow @fx @fy @fz
  if (@fx > 1100)
    set @fx = (@fx - 10)
  extern AI_SetXYZ hArrow @fx @fy @fz
  extern AI_GetRoll hArrow @froll
  if (@froll < 360)
    set @froll = (@froll + 5)
  extern AI_SetRoll hArrow @froll
}

finishswitch {
  extern AI_DestroyEntity hArrow
  unset hArrow
  extern stopsound battle/character_boots_com/boots_fat_screen_loop.wav
}
